# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
local max -> derivative goes from positive to negative, second derivative stays negative ^bCWd2en8

local min -> derivative goes from negative to positive, second derivative stays positive ^fDEOlinZ

point of inflection -> first derivative same sign but touches 0, second derivative change sign ^EORRm4LV
